Lactic acid bacteria (LAB) are an order of gram-positive, low-GC, acid-tolerant, generally nonsporulating, nonrespiring, either rod-shaped (bacilli) or spherical (cocci) bacteria that share common metabolic and physiological characteristics.

# EN:FISH TAXONOMY APPROACH
#
# For the en:fish ingredients a special approach to the taxonomy has been chosen:
# the latin fish species names are always the lowest child of a common fish name.
# These latin names are noted as en:and la:lines.
# The common fish names can not be trusted for correctly identifying the fish species.
# The same generic name is often used to (incorrectly) designate multiple fish species.

# Lecithin is a generic term to designate any group of yellow-brownish fatty substances occurring in animal and plant tissues,
# which are amphiphilic – they attract both water and fatty substances (and so are both hydrophilic and lipophilic),
# and are used for smoothing food textures, dissolving powders (emulsifying),
# homogenizing liquid mixtures, and repelling sticking materials.
